IMPORTANT PLEASE READ Texas Department of Motor Vehicles  Choosing a moverYou will have many choices when it comes to selecting a moving company If your mover isnt licensed to conduct moves in Texas you could risk losing your material possessions family heirlooms or other items of personal and irreplaceable value It is illegal for a mover to operate without a license to conduct moves You can
